RULES
table inet filter {
	chain input {
		type filter hook input priority filter; policy drop;
		iif "lo" accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.0/24 tcp dport 22 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 53 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp dport 53 accept
		ip protocol icmp accept
		tcp sport { 80, 443 }
		accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 53 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp sport 53 accept
		tcp dport 25 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 2049 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 2049 accept
	}

	chain forward {
		type filter hook forward priority filter; policy accept;
	}

	chain output {
		type filter hook output priority filter; policy drop;
		oif "lo" accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 53 accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp dport 53 accept
		tcp dport { 80, 443 } accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 53 accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp sport 53 accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.0/24 tcp sport 22 accept
		ip protocol icmp accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.133 tcp dport 25 accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 2049 accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 2049 accept
	}
}

#!/usr/sbin/nft -f

flush ruleset

table inet filter {
	chain input {
		type filter hook input priority filter; policy drop;
                iif lo accept
                ip saddr 192.168.3.0/24 tcp dport 22 accept;
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 53 accept;
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp dport 53 accept;
                ip protocol icmp accept;
                tcp sport { 80, 443}; accept;
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 53 accept;
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp sport 53 accept;
                tcp dport 25 accept;
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 2049 accept;                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 2049 accept;

	}
	chain forward {
		type filter hook forward priority filter;
	}
	chain output {
		type filter hook output priority filter; policy drop;
                oif lo accept
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 53 accept;
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp dport 53 accept;
                tcp dport { 80, 443} accept;
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 53 accept;
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp sport 53 accept;
                ip daddr 192.168.3.0/24 tcp sport 22 accept;
                ip protocol icmp accept;
                ip daddr 192.168.3.133 tcp dport 25 accept;
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 2049 accept;
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 2049 accept;
	}
}

table inet filter {
	chain input {
		type filter hook input priority filter; policy drop;
		iif "lo" accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.0/24 tcp dport 22 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 53 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp dport 53 accept
		ip protocol icmp accept
		tcp sport { 80, 443 } accept
		tcp sport 25 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 53 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp sport 53 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 25 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 25 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 2049 accept
		ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 2049 accept
	}

	chain forward {
		type filter hook forward priority filter; policy accept;
	}

	chain output {
		type filter hook output priority filter; policy drop;
		oif "lo" accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 53 accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp sport 53 accept
		tcp dport { 80, 443 } accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 53 accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp dport 53 accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.0/24 tcp sport 22 accept
		ip protocol icmp accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 25 accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 25 accept

		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 2049 accept
		ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 2049 accept
	}
}

table inet filter {
	chain input {
		type filter hook input priority filter; policy drop;
                iif lo accept
                ip saddr 192.168.3.0/24 tcp dport 22 accept;
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 53 accept;
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp dport 53 accept;
                ip protocol icmp accept;
                tcp sport { 80, 443} accept;
                tcp sport 25 accept
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 53 accept;
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp sport 53 accept;
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 25 accept;
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 25 accept;
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 2049 accept;                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 2049 accept;
	}
	chain forward {
		type filter hook forward priority filter;
	}
	chain output {
		type filter hook output priority filter; policy drop;
                oif lo accept
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 53 accept;
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp sport 53 accept;
                tcp dport { 80, 443} accept;
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 53 accept;

#!/usr/sbin/nft -f

flush ruleset

table inet filter {
	chain input {
		type filter hook input priority filter; policy drop;
                iif "lo" accept
                ip saddr 192.168.3.0/24 tcp dport 22 accept
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 53 accept
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp dport 53 accept
                ip protocol icmp accept
                tcp sport { 80, 443 } accept
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 53 accept
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp sport 53 accept
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 25 accept
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 25 accept
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 2049 accept
                ip saddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 2049 accept
	}
	chain forward {
		type filter hook forward priority filter;
	}
	chain output {
		type filter hook output priority filter; policy drop;
                oif "lo" accept
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 53 accept
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp sport 53 accept
                tcp dport { 80, 443 } accept
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 53 accept
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 udp dport 53 accept
                ip daddr 192.168.3.0/24 tcp sport 22 accept
                ip protocol icmp accept
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 25 accept
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 25 accept
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp sport 2049 accept
                ip daddr 192.168.3.128/25 tcp dport 2049 accept
	}
}
